`selectors::parser::SelectorImpl` trait for Braille's selector engine. This defines the string types and pseudo-class/pseudo-element types that our selector matching will use.\n\n**Files created:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/css/selector_impl.rs` -- `BrailleSelectorImpl` struct + trait impl + supporting types\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nDefine `BrailleSelectorImpl` as a unit struct that implements `selectors::parser::SelectorImpl`. The associated types are:\n\n- `ExtraMatchingData<'a>` = `()` (no extra data needed)\n- `AttrValue` = `String`\n- `Identifier` = `String` (but must impl `PrecomputedHash` -- wrap in a newtype `CssIdentifier(String)` that impls `PrecomputedHash`, `ToCss`, `Clone`, `Eq`, `From<&str>`)\n- `LocalName` = `CssLocalName(String)` newtype (impls `PrecomputedHash`, `ToCss`, `Clone`, `Eq`, `From<&str>`, `Borrow<str>`)\n- `NamespaceUrl` = `CssNamespaceUrl(String)` newtype (impls `PrecomputedHash`, `Clone`, `Eq`, `Default`, `Borrow<str>`)\n- `NamespacePrefix` = `CssNamespacePrefix(String)` newtype (impls `ToCss`, `Clone`, `Eq`, `From<&str>`, `Default`)\n- `BorrowedNamespaceUrl` = `str`\n- `BorrowedLocalName` = `str`\n- `NonTSPseudoClass` = `BraillePseudoClass` enum covering `:hover`, `:focus`, `:active`, `:visited`, `:link`, `:enabled`, `:disabled`, `:checked`, `:first-child`, `:last-child` (note: `:first-child` and `:last-child` are tree-structural and handled differently, but the selectors crate handles them internally -- only non-TS ones go here). Implement `selectors::parser::NonTSPseudoClass` trait on it (methods: `is_active_or_hover`, `is_user_action_state`) and `ToCss`.\n- `PseudoElement` = `BraillePseudoElement` enum covering `::before`, `::after`, `::placeholder`. Implement `selectors::parser::PseudoElement` trait and `ToCss`.\n\nAlso implement `selectors::parser::Parser` for a `BrailleSelectorParser` struct, which is needed by `SelectorList::parse`. This parser's `parse_non_ts_pseudo_class` and `parse_pseudo_element` methods convert CSS tokens into the respective enum variants.\n\n**Tests:**\n- Parse a simple selector like `div.foo` using `SelectorList::parse` with `BrailleSelectorParser` and verify it succeeds\n- Parse `#id`, `.class`, `h1 > p`, `a:hover`, `input:disabled`, `p::before`\n- Verify that invalid selectors produce errors\n- Round-trip test: parse a selector then serialize it back with `ToCss`\n\n**Depends on:** Nothing (only depends on the `selectors` crate)\n\n---\n\n### Agent 0C: DOM Modifications for Style Support\n\n**What it implements:** Adds the necessary infrastructure to `Node`/`DomTree` to support style attachment and attribute querying needed by the `selectors::Element` trait.\n\n**Files edited:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/dom/node.rs` -- add `style` field to `Node`, add `class_list()` and `get_attribute()` helper methods on element data\n- `/crates/engine/src/dom/tree.rs` -- add traversal helpers needed by `selectors::Element`: `parent_element()`, `prev_sibling_element()`, `next_sibling_element()`, `first_element_child()`, `is_root_element()`\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nIn `node.rs`:\n- Add to `Node`: `pub computed_style: Option<ComputedStyleIndex>` where `ComputedStyleIndex = usize` (or start with `Option<Box<ComputedStyle>>` if keeping it simpler; use a forward-declared type from `css` module via a type alias). For now, just add `pub inline_style: Option<Vec<(String, String)>>` -- a parsed inline style property-value list, and `pub computed_style: Option<usize>` as a placeholder index.\n- Add helper on `NodeData::Element` variant: method to get attribute by name (`get_attribute(&str) -> Option<&str>`). This is already partially possible via the `attributes` Vec but a direct method is cleaner.\n\nIn `tree.rs` add these traversal methods:\n- `parent_element(node_id: NodeId) -> Option<NodeId>` -- walks up to find first Element parent (skipping Document)\n- `prev_sibling_element(node_id: NodeId) -> Option<NodeId>` -- walks backward through parent's children to find previous Element sibling\n- `next_sibling_element(node_id: NodeId) -> Option<NodeId>` -- walks forward through parent's children to find next Element sibling\n- `first_element_child(node_id: NodeId) -> Option<NodeId>` -- first child that is an Element\n- `is_root_element(node_id: NodeId) -> bool` -- true if this element is the `<html>` element (child of Document)\n- `get_attribute(node_id: NodeId, name: &str) -> Option<String>` -- gets an attribute value from an element node\n\n**Tests:**\n- `parent_element` skips Document nodes, returns None at root\n- `prev_sibling_element` and `next_sibling_element` skip text nodes\n- `first_element_child` skips text nodes\n- `is_root_element` returns true for `<html>`, false for `<body>`\n- `get_attribute` retrieves correct values, returns None for missing attributes\n\n**Depends on:** Nothing\n\n---\n\n## Wave 1: Parsing + Matching (3 agents in parallel)\n\nAll depend on Wave 0 completing. These three are independent of each other.\n\n---\n\n### Agent 1A: CSS Stylesheet Parser\n\n**What it implements:** Uses `cssparser` to parse CSS text into a structured representation of rules (selector list + declarations).\n\n**Files created:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/css/parser.rs` -- `parse_stylesheet`, `parse_inline_style`, CssRule struct, supporting parser trait impls\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nDefine data structures:\n- `CssRule` struct: `selectors: SelectorList<BrailleSelectorImpl>`, `declarations: Vec<Declaration>`\n- `Declaration` struct: `property: PropertyId`, `value: CssValue`, `important: bool`\n- `Stylesheet` struct: `rules: Vec<CssRule>` (wraps a vec of rules)\n\nImplement the cssparser parser traits:\n\n`BrailleStyleSheetParser` struct implementing:\n- `QualifiedRuleParser<'i>` with `Prelude = SelectorList<BrailleSelectorImpl>`, `QualifiedRule = CssRule`, `Error = ()`:\n  - `parse_prelude`: use `SelectorList::parse(&BrailleSelectorParser, input)` to parse the selector\n  - `parse_block`: parse declarations inside `{ }` using a nested `BrailleDeclarationParser`\n- `AtRuleParser<'i>` with empty types (return error for all @-rules initially)\n- `RuleBodyItemParser<'i>` forwarding to the qualified rule parser\n\n`BrailleDeclarationParser` struct implementing:\n- `DeclarationParser<'i>` with `Declaration = Declaration`, `Error = ()`:\n  - `parse_value`: given a property name string, map to `PropertyId`, then parse the value tokens into a `CssValue`. Handle `!important` via `cssparser::parse_important`.\n- `AtRuleParser<'i>` with empty types (no at-rules inside blocks)\n- `RuleBodyItemParser<'i>` forwarding to declaration parser\n\nPublic functions:\n- `parse_stylesheet(css: &str) -> Stylesheet` -- creates `ParserInput`, `Parser`, iterates with `StyleSheetParser`\n- `parse_inline_style(style_attr: &str) -> Vec<Declaration>` -- parses declaration list from a `style=\"\"` attribute\n- `parse_value_for_property(property: PropertyId, value_str: &str) -> Option<CssValue>` -- utility for parsing a single property value\n\n**Tests:**\n- Parse `h1 { color: red; font-size: 16px; }` -- verify one rule with two declarations\n- Parse `div.foo > p { margin: 10px; }` -- verify selector parsed correctly, shorthand expanded\n- Parse inline style `\"color: blue; display: none\"` -- verify two declarations\n- Parse `!important` flag: `color: red !important` sets `important: true`\n- Parse multiple rules\n- Parse unknown properties gracefully (skip them)\n- Parse empty stylesheet returns empty rules vec\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 0A (PropertyId, CssValue), Agent 0B (BrailleSelectorImpl, BrailleSelectorParser)\n\n---\n\n### Agent 1B: Element Trait Implementation (Selector Matching)\n\n**What it implements:** The `selectors::Element` trait on a wrapper type that provides access to DomTree nodes for selector matching.\n\n**Files created:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/css/element_ref.rs` -- `DomElement` wrapper struct + `selectors::Element` impl\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nDefine `DomElement<'a>` struct:\n```\npub struct DomElement<'a> {\n    node_id: NodeId,\n    tree: &'a DomTree,\n}\n```\n\nThis is a lightweight, non-owning reference type. It holds a borrow of the DomTree and a NodeId. All trait methods delegate to `DomTree` traversal methods added by Agent 0C.\n\nImplement `selectors::Element` trait:\n- `type Impl = BrailleSelectorImpl`\n- `opaque()` -> `OpaqueElement::new(&self.node_id)` (use the NodeId as the identity -- needs to be stable, which it is since we use arena indices; might need a small wrapper since `OpaqueElement::new` takes `&T`)\n- `parent_element()` -> `self.tree.parent_element(self.node_id).map(|id| DomElement { node_id: id, tree: self.tree })`\n- `parent_node_is_shadow_root()` -> `false` (no shadow DOM)\n- `containing_shadow_host()` -> `None`\n- `is_pseudo_element()` -> `false`\n- `prev_sibling_element()` -> delegates to tree\n- `next_sibling_element()` -> delegates to tree\n- `first_element_child()` -> delegates to tree\n- `is_html_element_in_html_document()` -> `true` (we always parse HTML)\n- `has_local_name(name)` -> compare element tag_name against name\n- `has_namespace(ns)` -> compare against HTML namespace (or just return true for empty/HTML ns)\n- `is_same_type(other)` -> compare tag names\n- `attr_matches(ns, local_name, operation)` -> check element attributes using the AttrSelectorOperation enum\n- `match_non_ts_pseudo_class(pc, context)` -> for `:link`, check if element is `<a>` with href; for `:hover`/`:focus`/`:active`, return false (no user interaction state yet); for `:enabled`/`:disabled`/`:checked`, check element type + attributes\n- `match_pseudo_element(pe, context)` -> `false` (we don't render pseudo-elements)\n- `apply_selector_flags(flags)` -> no-op (we don't do invalidation yet)\n- `is_link()` -> check if `<a>` with `href` attribute\n- `is_html_slot_element()` -> `false`\n- `has_id(id, case_sensitivity)` -> check `id` attribute with appropriate case comparison\n- `has_class(name, case_sensitivity)` -> parse `class` attribute, check if name is in the space-separated list\n- `has_custom_state(name)` -> `false`\n- `imported_part(name)` -> `None`\n- `is_part(name)` -> `false`\n- `is_empty()` -> check if element has no element children and no non-empty text children\n- `is_root()` -> delegates to `tree.is_root_element(self.node_id)`\n- `add_element_unique_hashes(filter)` -> add id and class hashes to bloom filter\n\nAlso implement `Clone`, `PartialEq`, `Eq` on `DomElement`.\n\nProvide a public function:\n- `query_selector(tree: &DomTree, root: NodeId, selector_str: &str) -> Option<NodeId>` -- parses selector, walks descendants, returns first match\n- `query_selector_all(tree: &DomTree, root: NodeId, selector_str: &str) -> Vec<NodeId>` -- parses selector, walks descendants, returns all matches\n- `matches_selector_against_element(tree: &DomTree, node_id: NodeId, selector: &Selector<BrailleSelectorImpl>) -> bool` -- wraps `selectors::matching::matches_selector`\n\nThese `query_selector`/`query_selector_all` functions are also needed by Direction B (DOM API surface), making this a shared prerequisite.\n\n**Tests:**\n- Match `div` selector against a `<div>` element -> true\n- Match `.foo` against element with `class=\"foo bar\"` -> true\n- Match `#myid` against element with `id=\"myid\"` -> true\n- Match `div > p` with proper parent-child relationship -> true\n- Match `h1, h2` against an `<h1>` -> true\n- `query_selector` returns first match\n- `query_selector_all` returns all matches in document order\n- Match `a:link` against `<a href=\"...\">` -> true\n- Match fails for non-matching selectors\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 0B (BrailleSelectorImpl), Agent 0C (DOM traversal methods)\n\n---\n\n### Agent 1C: Stylesheet Collection\n\n**What it implements:** Walks the parsed DOM to collect all `<style>` element contents and inline `style=\"\"` attributes, producing a list of stylesheets plus a mapping of inline styles per element.\n\n**Files created:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/css/collect.rs` -- `collect_stylesheets`, `collect_inline_styles`\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nPublic functions:\n- `collect_stylesheets(tree: &DomTree) -> Vec<Stylesheet>` -- walks tree, finds all `<style>` elements, extracts their text content, parses each with `parse_stylesheet()`, returns the list in document order\n- `collect_inline_styles(tree: &DomTree) -> HashMap<NodeId, Vec<Declaration>>` -- walks tree, for each element with a `style` attribute, parses it with `parse_inline_style()`, returns mapping\n\nBoth functions do a single DFS walk. They can be combined into a single `StyleCollection` struct:\n```\npub struct StyleCollection {\n    pub author_sheets: Vec<Stylesheet>,\n    pub inline_styles: HashMap<NodeId, Vec<Declaration>>,\n}\n\npub fn collect_styles(tree: &DomTree) -> StyleCollection\n```\n\nAlso include a UA (User Agent) stylesheet as a hardcoded constant -- a baseline stylesheet with default styles for HTML elements (e.g., `display: block` for `div`, `p`, `h1`-`h6`; `display: inline` for `span`, `a`, `em`, `strong`; `display: list-item` for `li`; `font-weight: bold` for `b`, `strong`; `font-style: italic` for `i`, `em`; `display: none` for `head`, `script`, `style`, etc.). Parse this once at startup.\n\n**Tests:**\n- Collect from `<style>body { color: red; }</style>` -> one stylesheet with one rule\n- Collect from two `<style>` tags -> two stylesheets in order\n- Collect inline `<div style=\"color: blue\">` -> one entry in inline_styles map\n- Mixed: page with both `<style>` and inline styles\n- No styles at all -> empty collection\n- UA stylesheet parses without errors\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 0A (property/value types used by parser), Agent 1A (parse_stylesheet, parse_inline_style functions)\n\nNote: This agent technically depends on Agent 1A (the parser). If Agent 1A is not yet done, Agent 1C can define its interface/types first and write tests with inline-constructed `Stylesheet` objects, then wire up the real parser later. Alternatively, schedule Agent 1C in Wave 2. For maximum parallelism, have Agent 1C start at Wave 1 with the understanding it may need a short sync at the end.\n\n**Revised dependency:** Agent 1C depends on Agent 1A. Move to Wave 2 if strict ordering is needed, or let it start in parallel and finalize after 1A.\n\n---\n\n## Wave 2: Cascade Algorithm (2 agents in parallel)\n\nDepends on Wave 1 completing (parsing, matching, collection all ready).\n\n---\n\n### Agent 2A: Cascade Algorithm\n\n**What it implements:** The core cascade: for each element, collect all matching rules, sort by specificity + source order + importance, produce the \"cascaded value\" for each property.\n\n**Files created:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/css/cascade.rs` -- `cascade_element`, `CascadedValues`, specificity ordering\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nData structures:\n- `CascadedValues` = `HashMap<PropertyId, CascadedEntry>` where `CascadedEntry` = `{ value: CssValue, important: bool }`\n\nThe cascade algorithm for a single element:\n1. Start with an empty `CascadedValues` map\n2. Collect matching rules from all sources in order:\n   a. UA stylesheet (lowest priority)\n   b. Author stylesheets (in document order)\n   c. Inline style (highest normal priority)\n3. For each source, iterate over rules. For each rule, check if its selector matches the element using `matches_selector_against_element`. If it matches, for each declaration in that rule:\n   - Compute the \"order key\": (origin, importance, specificity, source_order)\n   - If this property is not yet in the map, or this declaration's order key beats the existing one, replace it\n4. Origin + importance ordering (per CSS spec):\n   - Normal UA < Normal Author < Normal Inline < Important Author < Important Inline < Important UA\n   - Within same origin+importance: sort by specificity, then source order (later wins)\n\nPublic functions:\n- `cascade_element(tree: &DomTree, node_id: NodeId, ua_sheet: &Stylesheet, author_sheets: &[Stylesheet], inline_styles: &HashMap<NodeId, Vec<Declaration>>) -> CascadedValues`\n\nImplementation detail: The `selectors::Selector::specificity()` method returns a `u32`. The cascade key is a tuple `(origin_importance_rank: u8, specificity: u32, source_order: u32)` compared lexicographically.\n\n**Tests:**\n- Single rule matching -> values appear in cascaded output\n- Two rules with same property -> higher specificity wins: `div { color: red; }` vs `div.foo { color: blue; }` on `<div class=\"foo\">` -> blue\n- Same specificity, later rule wins: two `div` rules in order\n- `!important` beats normal regardless of specificity\n- Inline style beats author stylesheet at normal importance\n- `!important` in author beats normal inline\n- UA stylesheet values appear when no author/inline overrides\n- Non-matching rules are excluded\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 1A (Stylesheet/Declaration types), Agent 1B (matches_selector_against_element), Agent 1C (StyleCollection)\n\n---\n\n### Agent 2B: Computed Style Resolution\n\n**What it implements:** Resolves cascaded values through inheritance and initial values to produce final computed styles. Handles `inherit`, `initial`, `unset` keywords, unit resolution (`em` -> `px`), and property inheritance.\n\n**Files created:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/css/computed.rs` -- `ComputedStyle` struct, `resolve_style`\n\n**Specifics:**\n\n`ComputedStyle` struct containing concrete computed values for every supported property:\n```\npub struct ComputedStyle {\n    pub display: Display,\n    pub visibility: Visibility,\n    pub color: CssColor,\n    pub background_color: CssColor,\n    pub font_size: f32,          // always in px\n    pub font_weight: u16,        // numeric 100-900\n    pub font_style: FontStyle,   // normal, italic, oblique\n    pub font_family: String,\n    pub line_height: f32,        // computed px or multiplier\n    pub margin_top: f32,         // px\n    pub margin_right: f32,\n    pub margin_bottom: f32,\n    pub margin_left: f32,\n    pub padding_top: f32,\n    pub padding_right: f32,\n    pub padding_bottom: f32,\n    pub padding_left: f32,\n    pub width: Option<f32>,      // None = auto\n    pub height: Option<f32>,\n    pub position: Position,      // static, relative, absolute, fixed, sticky\n    pub opacity: f32,\n    pub pointer_events: PointerEvents,\n    // ... additional properties as needed\n}\n```\n\nProvide `ComputedStyle::initial()` that returns the spec-defined initial values for all properties.\n\nResolution function:\n- `resolve_style(cascaded: &CascadedValues, parent_style: Option<&ComputedStyle>) -> ComputedStyle`\n  1. Start with `ComputedStyle::initial()`\n  2. For inherited properties: if no cascaded value, inherit from parent (or use initial if no parent)\n  3. For non-inherited properties: if no cascaded value, use initial value\n  4. For each cascaded value:\n     - `CssValue::Inherit` -> use parent's computed value\n     - `CssValue::Initial` -> use initial value\n     - `CssValue::Unset` -> if inherited property, inherit; otherwise initial\n     - `CssValue::Length(val, Em)` -> multiply by parent's (or current element's) font-size to get px\n     - `CssValue::Length(val, Rem)` -> multiply by root element's font-size to get px\n     - `CssValue::Percentage(pct)` -> context-dependent (font-size: % of parent font-size; width: % of containing block)\n     - `CssValue::Keyword(k)` for font-weight -> map `bold` to 700, `normal` to 400, `bolder`/`lighter` relative to parent\n     - Colors: resolve named colors to RGBA\n\n**Tests:**\n- Initial values are correct for all properties\n- Inherited property (color) passes from parent to child when no cascaded value\n- Non-inherited property (margin) uses initial value when no cascaded value\n- `inherit` keyword on non-inherited property forces inheritance\n- `initial` keyword on inherited property forces initial value\n- `em` units resolved: `2em` with parent `font-size: 16px` -> `32px`\n- `unset` on inherited property -> inherits; on non-inherited -> initial\n- `display: none` is correctly computed\n- `visibility: hidden` is correctly computed\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 0A (PropertyId, CssValue, PropertyMeta for inheritance flags), Agent 2A (CascadedValues)\n\n---\n\n## Wave 3: Style Tree + A11y Integration (3 agents in parallel)\n\nDepends on Wave 2 completing.\n\n---\n\n### Agent 3A: Style Computation Orchestration\n\n**What it implements:** The top-level function that walks the entire DOM tree and computes styles for every element, storing computed styles on the tree.\n\n**Files created:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/css/style.rs` -- `compute_all_styles`, `StyleContext`\n\n**Files edited:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/dom/node.rs` -- ensure the computed style storage field exists (may already be added by Agent 0C)\n- `/crates/engine/src/dom/tree.rs` -- add `set_computed_style(node_id, ComputedStyle)` and `get_computed_style(node_id) -> Option<&ComputedStyle>` methods\n\n**Specifics:**\n\n`StyleContext` struct:\n```\npub struct StyleContext {\n    pub ua_stylesheet: Stylesheet,\n    pub author_stylesheets: Vec<Stylesheet>,\n    pub inline_styles: HashMap<NodeId, Vec<Declaration>>,\n    pub computed_styles: Vec<Option<ComputedStyle>>,  // indexed by NodeId\n}\n```\n\n`compute_all_styles(tree: &mut DomTree, collection: &StyleCollection)`:\n1. Parse the UA stylesheet (hardcoded CSS string) -> `Stylesheet`\n2. DFS walk the tree in document order\n3. For each element node:\n   a. Get parent's computed style (if parent is an element)\n   b. Call `cascade_element()` to get cascaded values\n   c. Call `resolve_style()` with cascaded values + parent style\n   d. Store computed style on the node (via `tree.set_computed_style(node_id, style)`)\n4. Text nodes, comment nodes, document node: skip (no style)\n\nAlso provide:\n- `restyle_subtree(tree: &mut DomTree, node_id: NodeId, ...)` for incremental re-computation when inline styles change (needed for `element.style.setProperty()`)\n\n**Tests:**\n- Full tree computation: `<html><body><div style=\"color: red\"><p>text</p></div></body></html>` -> div gets `color: red`, p inherits `color: red`\n- `display: none` on an element -> computed style shows `Display::None`\n- Styles are computed in document order (parent before child, so inheritance works)\n- Elements without any matching rules get UA defaults\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 2A (cascade), Agent 2B (computed style resolution), Agent 1C (stylesheet collection)\n\n---\n\n### Agent 3B: A11y Integration (display:none + visibility:hidden)\n\n**What it implements:** Modifies the accessibility tree serializer to respect `display:none` (skip entirely) and `visibility:hidden` (preserve structure, hide text).\n\n**Files edited:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/a11y/serialize.rs` -- modify `walk` function to check computed styles\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nIn the `walk` function of `serialize_a11y`, before processing an Element node:\n1. Check if the element has a computed style\n2. If `display == Display::None`: return immediately (skip this element AND all its descendants -- do not recurse)\n3. If `visibility == Visibility::Hidden`: emit the role line but without text content. Still recurse into children (children may have `visibility: visible` which overrides).\n\nThe existing `SKIP_ELEMENTS` list (`head`, `script`, `style`, etc.) should remain -- those are always skipped regardless of CSS. The CSS `display:none` check is an additional filter.\n\nThis requires `serialize_a11y` to accept either a reference to the computed styles or have access to them through the `DomTree`. The cleanest approach: if computed styles are stored on the DomTree nodes (via the slot added by Agent 0C/3A), then `serialize_a11y` can read them directly.\n\nUpdate the function signature if needed: `serialize_a11y(tree: &DomTree) -> String` can remain the same if styles are stored on nodes. The `walk` function just checks `tree.get_computed_style(node_id)`.\n\n**Tests:**\n- Element with `display: none` is excluded from a11y output\n- Children of `display: none` element are also excluded\n- Element with `visibility: hidden` appears in structure but text is empty\n- Child of `visibility: hidden` with `visibility: visible` has its text shown\n- Existing tests continue to pass (no computed styles = no filtering, backward compatible)\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 3A (computed styles are stored on nodes)\n\nNote: This agent can start in parallel with 3A if it writes tests that manually set computed styles on nodes, then wire up to the real computation later. Or it can wait for 3A. For maximum parallelism, start it with Agent 3A and coordinate on the style storage API.\n\n---\n\n### Agent 3C: Engine Integration\n\n**What it implements:** Wires up style computation into the `Engine::load_html` pipeline so that after HTML parsing and script execution, styles are computed.\n\n**Files edited:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/lib.rs` -- add `pub mod css;`, call style computation in `load_html`\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nIn `Engine::load_html`, after executing scripts (step 3-4 in current flow), add:\n1. Collect styles: `let collection = css::collect::collect_styles(&self.tree.borrow())`\n2. Compute all styles: `css::style::compute_all_styles(&mut self.tree.borrow_mut(), &collection)`\n\nThis ensures that by the time `snapshot()` is called, all elements have computed styles, and the a11y serializer can read them.\n\nAlso add to `Engine`:\n- `pub fn restyle(&mut self)` -- re-collects and re-computes styles (for after JS mutations)\n- The `load_html` method already calls scripts before styling, which is correct\n\nUpdate `Cargo.toml` to add the new dependencies:\n```toml\ncssparser = \"0.36\"\nselectors = \"0.36\"\n```\n\n**Tests:**\n- End-to-end: HTML with `<style>div { display: none; }</style><div>hidden</div><p>visible</p>` -> a11y output shows only the paragraph\n- HTML with inline style: `<div style=\"visibility: hidden\">invisible</div>` -> structure but no text\n- Existing tests continue to pass\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 3A (compute_all_styles), Agent 3B (a11y integration)\n\n---\n\n## Wave 4: JS Bindings (2 agents in parallel)\n\nDepends on Wave 3 completing.\n\n---\n\n### Agent 4A: getComputedStyle() JS Binding\n\n**What it implements:** The `window.getComputedStyle(element)` JavaScript function that returns a CSSStyleDeclaration-like object.\n\n**Files edited:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/js/bindings.rs` -- add `getComputedStyle` registration + `JsCSSStyleDeclaration` class\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nDefine `JsCSSStyleDeclaration` as a Boa `Class`:\n```\nstruct JsCSSStyleDeclaration {\n    node_id: NodeId,\n    tree: Rc<RefCell<DomTree>>,\n    readonly: bool,  // true for getComputedStyle result, false for element.style\n}\n```\n\nThis class needs:\n- A `getPropertyValue(name)` method: looks up the computed style for the given property name, returns the CSS string representation\n- `length` getter: number of properties with values\n- `item(index)` method: return property name at index\n- Individual property accessors as getters on the prototype: `color`, `fontSize` (camelCase), `display`, etc. For the initial implementation, support the most commonly accessed properties via explicit getters. Later, can use a `Proxy` or dynamic property resolution.\n\nRegister `window.getComputedStyle` as a global function (or on a `window` object if one exists):\n```\nfn get_computed_style(this: &JsValue, args: &[JsValue], ctx: &mut Context) -> JsResult<JsValue>\n```\nThis function:\n1. Gets the element argument (a `JsElement`)\n2. Reads its `node_id`\n3. Creates a `JsCSSStyleDeclaration` with `readonly: true`, referencing the same tree\n4. Returns it as a JS object\n\nProperty name mapping: CSS `font-size` -> JS `fontSize` (camelCase). Implement both the camelCase accessors and `getPropertyValue(\"font-size\")` (kebab-case string).\n\n**Tests:**\n- `getComputedStyle(el).color` returns the computed color for an element\n- `getComputedStyle(el).display` returns computed display\n- `getComputedStyle(el).getPropertyValue(\"font-size\")` returns computed font-size\n- `getComputedStyle(el).fontSize` (camelCase) returns same as `getPropertyValue(\"font-size\")`\n- Returns correct inherited values\n- Throws or returns empty for non-element arguments\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 3A (computed styles stored on tree), existing JS binding infrastructure (Agent 0C from spike)\n\n---\n\n### Agent 4B: element.style JS Binding\n\n**What it implements:** The `element.style` property that returns a mutable CSSStyleDeclaration for reading/writing inline styles.\n\n**Files edited:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/js/bindings.rs` -- add `style` accessor on `JsElement`\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nAdd a `style` getter on the `JsElement` class (in `Class::init`):\n- Returns a `JsCSSStyleDeclaration` with `readonly: false` and `is_inline: true`\n- When `readonly: false`, writing to properties mutates the element's inline style in the DomTree\n\nThe mutable `JsCSSStyleDeclaration` needs additional methods:\n- `setProperty(name, value, priority?)` -- parses the value, updates the element's inline style attribute in the DomTree, triggers restyle\n- `removeProperty(name)` -- removes the property from inline style, triggers restyle\n- Property setters (camelCase): `el.style.color = \"red\"` -> equivalent to `setProperty(\"color\", \"red\")`\n\nWhen an inline style is modified:\n1. Update the `style` attribute on the DOM element\n2. Mark the element (and descendants) as needing restyle\n3. The restyle happens on the next `snapshot()` call or can be triggered immediately\n\nAlso implement the `style` attribute serialization: when reading `element.getAttribute(\"style\")`, it should return the serialized inline style string.\n\n**Tests:**\n- `el.style.color = \"red\"` sets inline style, reading it back returns `\"red\"`\n- `el.style.setProperty(\"font-size\", \"16px\")` works\n- `el.style.removeProperty(\"color\")` removes the property\n- `el.style.display = \"none\"` -> after restyle, element is hidden in a11y output\n- `el.style.getPropertyValue(\"color\")` returns the inline value\n- Setting a style and then calling `getComputedStyle` reflects the change\n\n**Depends on:** Agent 4A (JsCSSStyleDeclaration class -- shared with 4A, or defined independently and merged), existing JS binding infrastructure\n\n---\n\n## Wave 5: Final Integration + Edge Cases (1 agent)\n\nDepends on all of Wave 4.\n\n---\n\n### Agent 5A: Integration Tests + Edge Cases\n\n**What it implements:** End-to-end integration tests and edge case handling.\n\n**Files created/edited:**\n- `/crates/engine/src/css/mod.rs` -- ensure all submodules are properly exported\n- Integration tests in relevant test modules\n\n**Specifics:**\n\nWrite comprehensive integration tests:\n1. Full cascade test: HTML with UA styles + `<style>` + inline style + `!important` -> verify correct winner for each property\n2. Inheritance chain: `<html style=\"font-size:20px\"><body><div><p>text</p></div></body></html>` -> p inherits 20px font-size\n3. `display:none` in a11y: `<div style=\"display:none\"><p>hidden paragraph</p></div>` -> not in output\n4. `visibility:hidden`: structure preserved, text hidden\n5. JS interaction: script sets `el.style.display = \"none\"`, then snapshot excludes it\n6. `getComputedStyle` after JS mutation: script changes inline style, `getComputedStyle` reflects the cascaded result\n7. Specificity edge cases: id vs class vs element selectors\n8. Multiple `<style>` blocks, later one overrides\n9. `inherit` and `initial` keyword tests through JS\n10. Empty style blocks, malformed CSS (graceful handling)\n\nAlso handle these edge cases:\n- `<link rel=\"stylesheet\">` -- detect the element but note \"external stylesheets not yet supported\" (placeholder for future Direction A integration where network fetching exists)\n- Unknown CSS properties -- silently skip\n- Malformed CSS values -- silently skip the declaration\n- `@media` rules -- skip for now (no viewport concept yet)\n- `@import` -- skip for now (no network)\n\n**Tests:** All of the above integration tests.\n\n**Depends on:** All previous waves\n\n---\n\n## Wave Summary\n\n| Wave | Agents | Agent IDs | What | Depends On |\n|------|--------|-----------|------|------------|\n| 0 | 3 parallel | 0A, 0B, 0C | Property system, SelectorImpl types, DOM traversal helpers | Nothing |\n| 1 | 3 parallel | 1A, 1B, 1C | CSS parser, Element trait impl, Stylesheet collection | Wave 0 |\n| 2 | 2 parallel | 2A, 2B | Cascade algorithm, Computed style resolution | Wave 1 |\n| 3 | 3 parallel | 3A, 3B, 3C | Style tree orchestration, A11y integration, Engine wiring | Wave 2 |\n| 4 | 2 parallel | 4A, 4B | getComputedStyle() binding, element.style binding | Wave 3 |\n| 5 | 1 | 5A | Integration tests + edge cases | Wave 4 |\n\n**Total: 6 waves, 14 agent tasks, max 3 concurrent.**\n\n## Dependency Graph\n\n```\nWave 0:  [0A: Properties] [0B: SelectorImpl] [0C: DOM helpers]\n              |                   |                  |\n              v                   v                  v\nWave 1:  [1A: CSS Parser] [1B: Element trait] [1C: Collect styles]\n              |                   |                  |\n              +-------------------+------------------+\n              |\n              v\nWave 2:  [2A: Cascade]  [2B: Computed Style]\n              |                   |\n              +-------------------+\n              |\n              v\nWave 3:  [3A: Style Tree] [3B: A11y filter] [3C: Engine wire]\n              |                   |                  |\n              +-------------------+------------------+\n              |\n              v\nWave 4:  [4A: getComputedStyle] [4B: element.style]\n              |                        |\n              +------------------------+\n              |\n              v\nWave 5:  [5A: Integration tests]\n```\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n**1. Style storage on nodes:** Computed styles are stored directly on `Node` in the DomTree (as an `Option<Box<ComputedStyle>>`). This is simpler than a separate style tree and allows the a11y serializer to access styles without threading extra parameters.\n\n**2. DomElement wrapper type:** The `selectors::Element` trait is implemented on a non-owning `DomElement<'a>` wrapper that borrows the DomTree. This avoids Rc/RefCell complexity during matching -- we only need `&DomTree` for read-only traversal during matching, and the DomTree is not mutated during cascade computation (styles are accumulated separately, then written in one pass).\n\n**3. Cascade before storing:** The cascade for the entire tree runs in one pass (DFS), computing and storing styles top-down. This ensures parent styles are available when resolving child styles (needed for inheritance and em-unit resolution).\n\n**4. Restyle strategy:** After JS mutations to inline styles, a full restyle is triggered. This is simple and correct. Incremental restyle (dirty flags, subtree invalidation) is a future optimization.\n\n**5. UA stylesheet as hardcoded CSS:** The user-agent stylesheet is a const string of CSS that gets parsed once. This is clean and maintainable -- adding new default styles just means editing the CSS string.\n\n**6. Property system as enum:** Using a Rust enum for `PropertyId` rather than strings makes pattern matching exhaustive and prevents typos. The tradeoff is that adding new properties requires updating the enum, but this is a good forcing function for ensuring all properties are properly handled.\n\n## Cross-Direction Dependencies\n\nThis plan creates shared infrastructure useful for other directions:\n\n- **Direction B (DOM API):** Agent 1B's `query_selector`/`query_selector_all` functions are directly usable for `document.querySelector`/`querySelectorAll` JS bindings. The `BrailleSelectorImpl` and `DomElement` types are prerequisites.\n- **Direction A (Sessions):** External `<link rel=\"stylesheet\">` loading depends on the session/network layer from Direction A. The placeholder in Agent 5A marks where this integration point is.\n\n### Critical Files for Implementation\n- `/Users/danielkim/sandbox/tools/text-browser/crates/engine/src/css/element_ref.rs` - Core of selector matching: implements `selectors::Element` trait, enables querySelector and the entire cascade to work\n- `/Users/danielkim/sandbox/tools/text-browser/crates/engine/src/css/cascade.rs` - The cascade algorithm itself: collects matching rules, sorts by specificity/origin/order, produces cascaded values per element\n- `/Users/danielkim/sandbox/tools/text-browser/crates/engine/src/css/parser.rs` - CSS parsing via cssparser: turns CSS text into structured rules (selector + declarations), implements DeclarationParser and QualifiedRuleParser traits\n- `/Users/danielkim/sandbox/tools/text-browser/crates/engine/src/dom/tree.rs` - Must be extended with traversal helpers (parent_element, prev_sibling_element, etc.) and computed style storage that the Element trait impl delegates to\n- `/Users/danielkim/sandbox/tools/text-browser/crates/engine/src/js/bindings.rs` - Where getComputedStyle() and element.style bindings are added, making CSS visible to JavaScript"}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":451,"cache_read_input_tokens":71873,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":451},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"}},"requestId":"req_011CYwWD1woMtyfmof2Wr7yx","type":"assistant","uuid":"3df34905-7d72-445b-8d61-535798766a66","timestamp":"2026-03-11T15:13:11.391Z"}
